99 I need an expert in mobile, vpn and proxy networks who can help me setup a mobile proxy service where devices in other areas can login to my mobile hotspot to get a mobile IP read this for more details: To enable remote servers to access your hotspot, you need to configure port forwarding, static IP (or dynamic DNS), and firewall rules. The exact setup depends on the hotspot device and your carrier. ⸻ 1️⃣ Check Carrier Restrictions Some mobile carriers block inbound connections, preventing remote access. ✅ Check if your carrier: • Allows port forwarding • Provides a public IP address (Some use CGNAT, which blocks remote access) • If they block direct access, use VPN or reverse tunneling (see below). ⸻ 2️⃣ Enable Port Forwarding (If Supported) Many mobile hotspots (Netgear, Teltonika, Inseego, etc.) support port forwarding. How to Enable Port Forwarding on a Hotspot Router 1. Login to Router Admin Page • Open a browser and go to http://192.168.1.1 (or your router’s IP). • Enter admin credentials. 2. Find Port Forwarding Settings • Look under Advanced Settings → Port Forwarding / NAT. 3. Add a Port Forwarding Rule • Example settings: • Internal IP: 192.168.1.100 (device you want to expose) • External Port: 8080 (choose any open port) • Internal Port: 80 (or any port the service is running on) • Protocol: TCP 4. Save Restart Router 🔹 Now, your server should be accessible via: http://[Your Public IP]:8080 📌 To check your public IP: https://www.whatismyip.com ⸻ 3️⃣ Handle Dynamic IPs (Use Dynamic DNS) Most ISPs change public IP addresses periodically. Use a Dynamic DNS (DDNS) service like: ✅ Free DDNS providers: • No-IP • DynDNS • DuckDNS Steps to set up DDNS: 1. Register a free hostname (e.g., myhotspot.no-ip.com). 2. Configure DDNS in your router settings. 3. Use your DDNS hostname instead of your IP (http://myhotspot.no-ip.com:8080). ⸻ 4️⃣ Firewall Configuration (Open Ports) Some hotspot routers block incoming connections. Ensure your firewall allows remote access. For Netgear, Teltonika, Inseego Hotspots 1. Go to Firewall Settings (http://192.168.1.1) 2. Find Security / Firewall Rules. 3. Add an **Allow https://www.whatismyip.com Setup a Mobile Hotspot Proxy Server I can configure your mobile hotspot for remote access, following all steps outlined: port forwarding, dynamic DNS setup, and firewall adjustments.
